                  <div class="hidden-sm-down">
                   <h4 class="heading-3 heading-lg-2 padding-2" data-qa="model-search-default-heading">
                    The TruePrice Difference
                   </h4>
                   <ul class="list-bulleted spacing-2 padding-1">
                    <li class="_1s9zbcj font-size-3" data-qa="HomeLoader">
                     <div class="theme-bright spacing-1">
                      <h4 class="heading-4 heading-lg-3" data-qa="Heading">
                       A Better Price
                      </h4>
                      <p class="no-left-padding font-size-2">
                       With TrueCar, a certified dealer gives you an upfront, discounted price that includes all fees, accessory costs, and incentives. This is your TruePricethe price youll pay at the dealership.
                      </p>
                     </div>
                    </li>
                    <li class="_1s9zbcj font-size-3" data-qa="HomeLoader">
                     <div class="theme-bright spacing-1">
                      <h4 class="heading-4 heading-lg-3" data-qa="Heading">
                       Compare. Select. Save.
                      </h4>
                      <p class="no-left-padding font-size-2">
                       TruePrice is better because over 12,000 dealers uniquely set the price in TrueCar knowing you will see their prices alongside what other people paid. They price to get your business.
                      </p>
                     </div>
                    </li>
                    <li class="_1s9zbcj font-size-3" data-qa="HomeLoader">
                     <div class="theme-bright spacing-1">
                      <h4 class="heading-4 heading-lg-3" data-qa="Heading">
                       A Price Curve for EveryCar
                      </h4>
                      <p class="no-left-padding font-size-2">
                       Every new vehicle on TrueCar has a unique price curve that shows you what your neighbors paid for that same car. Cut through the clutter by instantly comparing the TruePrice to what other people paid.
                      </p>
                     </div>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
